Thus the root folder of archive will be displayed as an icon associated with archives of that type.\r\nAX-ZIP Extractor working space is made up of two windows - Archive Browser and File Browser.\r\nArchive Browser contains a tree representing the structure of disks, folders and archives - files with extension of supported archive types.
